The Supreme Court of the United States-is the only court ahaa by the
Constitution and is the court of last-resort. The Supreme Court has original
jurisdiction over all disputes involving foreign ministers and interstate
disputes, and disputes between the federal and state governments. The
Court has jurisdiction of cases originating from any other court if the case
involves constitutional issues, federal laws or maritime treaties and laws.:
The Supreme Court may affirm, modify, reverse or remand a decision ofa a
lower court. The Supreme Court is comprised of the Chief Justice and
eight associate justices, who are appointed by the President and confirmed
by the Senate. Among his or her responsibilities, each Justice is. assigned
to serve as “Circuit Justice” for one or more of the United States Judicial
Circuits. :

Judicial Yellow Book

  

United States Courts of
Appeals

Internet: app.comm.uscourts.gov/appeals.him

The intermediate appellate courts in the federal judicial system are the
courts of appeals. Twelve of these courts have jurisdiction over cases from
certain geographic areas. The Court of Appeals for the Federal Circuit has

: ational jurisdiction over specific types cf cases. A disappointed party in a

district court usually has the right to have the case reviewed in the court of
appeals for the circuit. Appeals court judges are appointed for life by the

: president with the advice and consent of the Senate. Each court of appeals

consists of six or more judges, depending on the caseload of the court. The
judge who has served on the court the longest and who is under 65 years —
of age is designated as the chief judge and performs administrative duties
in addition to hearing cases.

United States Court of Appeals for
the Federal Circuit

Howard T. Markey National Courts Building, 717 Madison Place, NW,.

Washington, DC 20439

Tel: (202) 633-6550 Tel: (202) 786-6584 (Electronic Opinions Data)
Tel: (202) 633-9608 (Electronic Opinions Data) “-

Tel: (202) 633-6550 (Electronic Opimigns Noles) Fax: (202) 633- 9623

Internet: www.fedciz.gov

Number of Judgeships: 12
Supreme Court Justice: Chief Justice tai G Roberts a.

The United States Court of Appeals for the Federal Circuit handles. cases
by subject matter -without-regard to the region. The Court hears all appeals
for the United States Court of Federal Claims, the United States Court of
International Trade and the United States Court of Veterans Appeals, The
Federal Circuit hears appeals from United States District Courts in patent-
cases, cases involving energy regulation and economic stabilization as well
as appeals from a variety of administrative proceedings. Established i in
1982, the Washington, DC-based Federal Circuit possesses national ©
jurisdiction as @ result of the merger between the Appellate Division of the
former United States Court of Claims and the United States Court of
Customs and Patent Appeals.

FEDERAL GCOURTS—UNITED STATES DISTRICT COURTS.

8&6 United States District Courts

United States District Courts

Most federal cases are initially tried and decided in the United States 04
District Courts, the federal courts of general trial jurisdiction. There a
courts in the 50 states, the District of Columbia, the Commonwealth 9 i
Puerto Rico, and the territories of Guam, the United States Virgin a 3»
and the Northern Mariana Islands. With the exception of the terior -
courts, all district court judges are appointed for life by the Exaile ne
the advice and consent of the Senate, In each district, the judge no
served on the court the longest and who is under 65 years of age i sea it
designated as the chief judge. The chief judge has administrative a *
addition to a caseload, Within each district, the United States Ba: Ey y¥
Court hears and decides petitions of individuals and businesses sec Top
relief from bankruptcy. Bankruptcy judges are appointed by feo ee
appeals for a term of 14 years. The judges of each district oa on i
more magistrate judges, who discharge many of the ancillary ta “ee
district judges. There are both full-time and part-time magistrate ae ne
positions, and these positions are assigned to the district courts = Sail

to caseload criteria. A full-time magistrate judge serves a term of CE
years; a part-time magistrate judge’s term is four years.
